##### THE KINGDOM OF GONDOR	#####		

#### Empire of Gondor ####		
e_gondor = {
	3912.1.1 = {
		holder = lineofanarion1 # Anárion 
		effect = {
			title:e_gondor.holder ?= {
				set_realm_capital = title:c_osgiliath
			}
			set_capital_county = title:c_osgiliath
		}
		government = administrative_government
		succession_laws = {
			acclamation_succession_law
		}
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					holder = { has_government = administrative_government }
				}
				set_state_faith = faith:faith_edain
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					has_dlc_feature = royal_court
				}
				holder = {
					set_court_type = court_diplomatic
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = holder
					NOT = { has_dlc_feature = roads_to_power }
				}
				holder = {
					change_government = feudal_government
					add_realm_law_skip_effects = single_heir_succession_law
				}
			}
		}
	}
	4032.4.17 = {
		holder = lineisildur0 # Isildur 
	}
	4035.10.5 = {
		holder = lineofanarion5 # Meneldil 
	}
	4191.8.2 = {
		holder = lineofanarion7 # Cemendur 
	}
	4271.11.20 = {
		holder = lineofanarion8 # Eärendil 
	}
	4357.8.23 = {

	}

	}

    }
